DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 \
      g++-14 \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git \
      wget \
      ca-certificates
  # Set default compiler to GCC 14
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
      && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100
  # Install Google Test
  RUN git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake . \
      && make install
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/facebook_zstd
  # Copy project files
  COPY . .
  # Build project
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja \
      && cmake --build build --parallel
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/facebook_zstd /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
      && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100
  # Install Google Test
  RUN git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake . \
      && make install
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /project
  # Copy project files
  COPY . .
  # Build project
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja \
      && cmake --build build --parallel
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 2 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      ca-certificates \
      wget \
      gnupg
  RUN wget -O - https://apt.kitware.com/keys/kitware-archive-latest.asc 2>/dev/null | gpg --dearmor - | tee /etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/kitware.gpg >/dev/null
  RUN apt-add-repository 'deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ jammy main' \
      && apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-13 \
      g++-13 \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-13 100 \
      && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-13 100
  RUN git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake . \
      && make install
  WORKDIR /project
  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja \
      && cmake --build build --parallel
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      ca-certificates \
      wget \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      && wget -O - https://apt.kitware.com/keys/kitware-archive-latest.asc 2>/dev/null | gpg --dearmor - | tee /etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/kitware.gpg >/dev/null \
      && echo "deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ $(lsb_release -cs) main" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/kitware.list \
      && apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-13 \
      g++-13 \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git \
      && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-13 100 \
      && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-13 100 \
      && git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake -B build -S . -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      && cmake --build build --parallel \
      && cmake --install build
  WORKDIR /project
  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      -DCMAKE_VERBOSE_MAKEFILE=ON \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_TESTS=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_CONTRIB=OFF \
      && cmake --build build --parallel --verbose
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      ca-certificates \
      wget \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      && apt-key adv --fetch-keys https://apt.kitware.com/keys/kitware-archive-latest.asc \
      && echo "deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ $(lsb_release -cs) main" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/kitware.list \
      && apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-13 \
      g++-13 \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git \
      && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-13 100 \
      && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-13 100 \
      && git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake -B build -S . -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      && cmake --build build --parallel \
      && cmake --install build
  WORKDIR /project
  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      -DCMAKE_VERBOSE_MAKEFILE=ON \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_TESTS=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_CONTRIB=OFF \
      && cmake --build build --parallel --verbose
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake -B build -S . -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      && cmake --build build --parallel \
      && cmake --install build

  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      -DCMAKE_VERBOSE_MAKEFILE=ON \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_TESTS=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_CONTRIB=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_PROGRAMS=ON \
      && cmake --build build --parallel --verbose
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      ca-certificates \
      wget \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      && wget -O - https://apt.kitware.com/keys/kitware-archive-latest.asc 2>/dev/null | gpg --dearmor - | tee /etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/kitware.gpg >/dev/null \
      && echo "deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ $(lsb_release -cs) main" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/kitware.list \
      && apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc \
      g++ \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git \
      && git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake -B build -S . -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      && cmake --build build --parallel \
      && cmake --install build
  WORKDIR /project
  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      -DCMAKE_VERBOSE_MAKEFILE=ON \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_TESTS=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_CONTRIB=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_PROGRAMS=ON \
      && cmake --build build --parallel --verbose
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 10 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      ca-certificates \
      wget \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      && wget -O - https://apt.kitware.com/keys/kitware-archive-latest.asc 2>/dev/null | gpg --dearmor - | tee /etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/kitware.gpg >/dev/null \
      && echo "deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ $(lsb_release -cs) main" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/kitware.list \
      && apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc \
      g++ \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git \
      && git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake -B build -S . -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      && cmake --build build --parallel \
      && cmake --install build
  WORKDIR /project
  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      -DCMAKE_VERBOSE_MAKEFILE=ON \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_TESTS=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_CONTRIB=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_PROGRAMS=ON \
      -DBUILD_SHARED_LIBS=ON \
      -DCMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX=/usr/local \
      -DCMAKE_C_FLAGS="-Wno-error" \
      -DCMAKE_CXX_FLAGS="-Wno-error" \
      && cmake --build build --parallel --verbose \
      && cmake --install build
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && ldconfig \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  ENV LD_LIBRARY_PATH="/usr/local/lib:${LD_LIBRARY_PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 12 ---

      -DCMAKE_CXX_FLAGS="-Wno-error -Wno-deprecated-declarations" \
      && cmake --build build --parallel --verbose 2>&1 | tee build_log.txt \
      && cmake --install build 2>&1 | tee install_log.txt
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  COPY --from=builder /project/build_log.txt /build_log.txt

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      software-properties-common \
      ca-certificates \
      wget \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      && wget -O - https://apt.kitware.com/keys/kitware-archive-latest.asc 2>/dev/null | gpg --dearmor - | tee /etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/kitware.gpg >/dev/null \
      && echo "deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ $(lsb_release -cs) main" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/kitware.list \
      && apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc \
      g++ \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git \
      && git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake -B build -S . -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      && cmake --build build --parallel \
      && cmake --install build
  WORKDIR /project
  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      -DCMAKE_VERBOSE_MAKEFILE=ON \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_TESTS=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_CONTRIB=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_PROGRAMS=ON \
      -DBUILD_SHARED_LIBS=ON \
      -DCMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX=/usr/local \
      -DCMAKE_C_FLAGS="-Wno-error -Wno-deprecated-declarations -v" \
      -DCMAKE_CXX_FLAGS="-Wno-error -Wno-deprecated-declarations -v" \
      && cmake --build build --parallel --verbose 2>&1 | tee build_log.txt \
      && cmake --install build 2>&1 | tee install_log.txt
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  COPY --from=builder /project/build_log.txt /build_log.txt
  COPY --from=builder /project/install_log.txt /install_log.txt
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && ldconfig \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  ENV LD_LIBRARY_PATH="/usr/local/lib:${LD_LIBRARY_PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 14 ---

      software-properties-common \
      ca-certificates \
      wget \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      && wget -O - https://apt.kitware.com/keys/kitware-archive-latest.asc 2>/dev/null | gpg --dearmor - | tee /etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/kitware.gpg >/dev/null \
      && echo "deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ $(lsb_release -cs) main" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/kitware.list \
      && apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc \
      g++ \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      python3 \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git \
      && git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake -B build -S . -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      && cmake --build build --parallel \
      && cmake --install build
  WORKDIR /project
  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      -DCMAKE_VERBOSE_MAKEFILE=ON \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_TESTS=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_CONTRIB=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_PROGRAMS=ON \
      -DBUILD_SHARED_LIBS=ON \
      -DCMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX=/usr/local \
      -DCMAKE_C_FLAGS="-Wno-error -Wno-deprecated-declarations -Wno-stringop-overflow -Wno-restrict -Wno-unused-parameter" \
      -DCMAKE_CXX_FLAGS="-Wno-error -Wno-deprecated-declarations -Wno-stringop-overflow -Wno-restrict -Wno-unused-parameter" \
      -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=RelWithDebInfo \
      && cmake --build build --parallel 2>&1 | tee build_log.txt \
      && cmake --install build 2>&1 | tee install_log.txt
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  COPY --from=builder /project/build_log.txt /build_log.txt
  COPY --from=builder /project/install_log.txt /install_log.txt
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && ldconfig \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  ENV LD_LIBRARY_PATH="/usr/local/lib:${LD_LIBRARY_PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 16 ---

      python3-pip \
      zlib1g-dev \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-dev \
      git \
      && git clone https://github.com/google/googletest.git /googletest \
      && cd /googletest \
      && cmake -B build -S . -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      && cmake --build build --parallel \
      && cmake --install build
  WORKDIR /project
  COPY . .
  RUN cmake -B build -S . -G Ninja -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \
      -DCMAKE_VERBOSE_MAKEFILE=ON \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_TESTS=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_CONTRIB=OFF \
      -DZSTD_BUILD_PROGRAMS=ON \
      -DBUILD_SHARED_LIBS=ON \
      -DCMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX=/usr/local \
      -DCMAKE_C_FLAGS="-Wno-error -Wno-deprecated-declarations -Wno-stringop-overflow -Wno-restrict -Wno-unused-parameter" \
      -DCMAKE_CXX_FLAGS="-Wno-error -Wno-deprecated-declarations -Wno-stringop-overflow -Wno-restrict -Wno-unused-parameter" \
      -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=RelWithDebInfo \
      && cmake --build build \
      && cmake --install build
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  COPY --from=builder /project /project
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local /usr/local
  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && ldconfig \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  ENV LD_LIBRARY_PATH="/usr/local/lib:${LD_LIBRARY_PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  WORKDIR /project
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      libstdc++6 \
      zlib1g \
      liblzma-dev \
      liblz4-1 \
      && ldconfig \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  ENV PATH="/project/build/programs:${PATH}"
  ENV LD_LIBRARY_PATH="/usr/local/lib:${LD_LIBRARY_PATH}"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 20 ---
